translate_to_node 呼叫compile.js 裡面的codegen函式 把compile.js自己的source code當作參數 自己解析自己

得到一個自動生成的c語言檔 compiler_code.c(裡面的東西是 compile.js(

```js
'use strict';

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////// PARSING



var charIsInRange = function (arg) {
    var lower = arg[0];
    var c = arg[1]; // falsy if eof
    var upper = arg[2];
    return c &&
           lower.charCodeAt(0) <= c.charCodeAt(0) &&
           c.charCodeAt(0) <= upper.charCodeAt(0);
};


///........ 省略了內容 完整的請看 compile.js

// Returns a list of compiled functions.
var codegen = function (statements) {
    //console.log(statements);
    var root = {
        type: 'function',
        children: statements,
        param: {type: 'null'}
    };

    // Assign an unique `_id` property to each function. The first function
    // must be the entrypoint.
    var functions = getFunctions(root);
    var i = 0;
    while (i < functions.length) {
        functions[i]._id = i;
        i = i + 1;
    }

    var compiledFuncs = [];
    i = 0;
    while (i < functions.length) {
        var func = functions[i];
        var compiled = compileFunctionBody(func.children);
        if (func.param.type !== 'null') {
            compiled.paramName = func.param.string;
        }
        compiledFuncs.push(compiled);
        i = i + 1;
    }
    //console.log(compiledFuncs);
    return compiledFuncs;
};


module.exports = function (source) {
    return codegen(parse(source));
};

```



 )裡的所有東西 只是變成 opcode的形式)

像是可以看到 func0 是所有的全域的東西(可以和上面比對)

而如果是那個const是函式呢, 裡面的內容不就看不見?

在compile.js 跑parse() 時, 他就會把函式的內容拿出來 放在下一個func

```
{// all the global var (函示的內部沒有)
```

而func1 就是compile.js 遇到的第一個函式

```js
var charIsInRange = function (arg) {
    var lower = arg[0];
    var c = arg[1]; // falsy if eof
    var upper = arg[2];
    return c &&
           lower.charCodeAt(0) <= c.charCodeAt(0) &&
           c.charCodeAt(0) <= upper.charCodeAt(0);
};
```

有了以上的opcode 

 compiler_code.c  get_builtin_file()  會依照func裡的bconst的數字或字串 創造object類型為string的value_t或是object 類型為number的value_t  最後把所有創造好的 value_t 放在consts陣列裡 把每個函式(75個)都consts都裝好後 回傳file的位置 來達到回傳全部75個函式 因為 file裡面的funcs是陣列的第一個位置 可以用這個位置來去找其他函式

```c
/////////////bvalue.c
static value_t bvalue_to_v(bvalue_t b) {
    switch (b.type) {
    case bvalue_type_string: return v_string(b.string); //new string object and link itself in big_link_list
    case bvalue_type_number: return v_number(b.number); //(double) number = b.number(didn't link in big_link_list)
    }
    abort();//error handling
}
void bvalue_array_to_v(value_t *v, const bvalue_t *b, size_t length) {
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        v[i] = bvalue_to_v(b[i]);
    }
}
//////////////compiler_code.c
static compiled_file_t file = {
  .func_count = 75,
  .funcs = (compiled_func_t[75]){},
};

compiled_file_t *get_builtin_file(void) {
  compiled_func_t funcs[75] = {func0, func1, func2, func3, func4, func5, func6, func7, func8, func9, func10, func11, func12, func13, func14, func15, func16, func17, func18, func19, func20, func21, func22, func23, func24, func25, func26, func27, func28, func29, func30, func31, func32, func33, func34, func35, func36, func37, func38, func39, func40, func41, func42, func43, func44, func45, func46, func47, func48, func49, func50, func51, func52, func53, func54, func55, func56, func57, func58, func59, func60, func61, func62, func63, func64, func65, func66, func67, func68, func69, func70, func71, func72, func73, func74, };

  memmove(file.funcs, funcs, sizeof(funcs));
  for (int i = 0; i < 75; i++) {
    compiled_func_t *func = file.funcs + i;
    bvalue_array_to_v(func->consts, func->bconsts, func->const_count);
  }
  return &file;
}
```

```c
compiled_file_t *get_builtin_file(void) {
  compiled_func_t funcs[75] = {func0, func1, func2, func3, func4, func5, func6, func7, func8, func9, func10, func11, func12, func13, func14, func15, func16, func17, func18, func19, func20, func21, func22, func23, func24, func25, func26, func27, func28, func29, func30, func31, func32, func33, func34, func35, func36, func37, func38, func39, func40, func41, func42, func43, func44, func45, func46, func47, func48, func49, func50, func51, func52, func53, func54, func55, func56, func57, func58, func59, func60, func61, func62, func63, func64, func65, func66, func67, func68, func69, func70, func71, func72, func73, func74, };

  memmove(file.funcs, funcs, sizeof(funcs));
  for (int i = 0; i < 75; i++) {
    compiled_func_t *func = file.funcs + i;
    bvalue_array_to_v(func->consts, func->bconsts, func->const_count);
  }
  return &file;
}
```
